JOHNSON WINS EVERY STATE AFTER GOLDWATER DROPS OUT! AUH20 CENSURED BY GOP!

You know, Barry, you may have made some misguided choices in your campaign, but you really stuck to your principles in the end.

Back in July, when you promised to drop out if anyone committed racial violence in your name, most thought you were bluffing. Everyone presumed it was to convince one wing of the party or the other to lighten up on racial issues.

Yet, here we are, with you having removed your name from the race only two days prior to the election.

It started on October 31st, when a white man from Waynesboro Mississippi was arrested for attacking an African American out trick or treating with his family.

The African American in question was fine, in the end, only a few stitches, and his family was perfectly fine too, but when the suspect was questioned about his motives, his official statement was “I’m helping President Goldwater restore order to this nation.”

The story was quickly picked up by several news outlets. Then, November First, Johnson himself challenged you on it in a public speech. Your campaign looked into it, and the suspect had been a registered Democrat up until the signing of the CRA, before switching his registration to Republican. You knew it was likely a plant, you knew President Johnson was baiting you, but reading those words over and over, you could feel something bubbling up inside you.The party was furious, of course. Two days was simply not enough time to field a new candidate. Across the nation, many were instructed to disregard your name on the ballot, something which was scrutinized heavily by conservative pundits, but no matter. What was done was done.

1964 saw record high third party votes. It also saw the first unanimous election since 1820. Still, without a party and without a job, the legacy you would leave behind was a positive, if not a bit impulsive, one.

Thank you, Senator Goldwater, for your bravery, and thank you for bringing about a new dawn in America.

BARRY GOLDWATER: DEFENDER OF CAPITALISM AND DESTROYER OF THE SOVIET UNION, WINS IN COMPLETE SWEEP!

It was days after the debate, when you headed out to an old air strip in Yuma County, Arizona, and chartered a plane.

“Enough of this. The world doesn’t have time for this. I’m not just going to win the election, I’m going to win the freedom of the whole damn world. And they thought I was joking!”

You spend the afternoon rigging the plane with everything you needed. Plenty of gas, a map, and of course, the Tactical Nuclear Warhead you’d held onto ever since the war had ended. You didn’t know if or when you’d be needing it, but just as your heart had never led you wrong before, you felt that now the time was right.

So off you went. For more than 12 hours, you flew, across the pacific, across the russian wilderness, until finally, Moscow was underfoot.

The map you had wasn’t perfect, but after a few passes over the Kremlin, you were pretty sure you could pinpoint the location of the mens room. You checked your watch. An old war buddy had managed to do some snooping for you, and you had it on good authority that at 3PM every day, Brezhnev would go to take a leak.

With a gulp of liquid luck, you passed overhead of the Kremlin. Then: Bombs Away.

You returned home a hero. The head of the snake had been cut off, and the rest of the body was quickly dying. The Russians were, somehow, incapable of gathering themselves enough to retaliate. Despite Johnson’s flaccid attempts to have the UN arrest you for violating the Geneva convention, in the ensuing election, America thanked you for your service.
